<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">around</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zet.html>zet</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to set, put</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***ondankbaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ondankbaar.html>ondankbaar</a> (10027)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">on-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">un-</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dankbaar.html>dankbaar</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thankful, grateful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondankbaar.html>ondankbaar</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondankbaar.html>ondankbaarder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">ondankbaarst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ungrateful, showing no gratitude
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>Wees</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ondankbaar.html>ondankbaar</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plezier.html>plezier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> be so ungrateful when someone does you a favor.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thankless, yielding (little or) no <a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>thanks</a> or reward; unproductive

***onder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> (253)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">under</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*under</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">undar</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:unter.html>unter</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">under</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>under, downwards</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">postpositional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (to) under (implying motion).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> <b>under</b> the car just like that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***onderbaas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderbaas.html>onderbaas</a> (33172)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">under</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:baas.html>baas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boss</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbaas.html>onderbaas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbazen.html>onderbazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbaas.html>onderbaasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">onderbazin</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a generic term referring to a person that <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a> on behalf of their <span class="Latn" lang="en">superior</span> in the event of the <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> superior's absence, such as an <span class="Latn" lang="en">acting</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">manager</span> of a <span class="Latn" lang="en">firm</span>; a <span class="Latn" lang="en">deputy</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">lieutenant</span></li>
<li>an <span class="Latn" lang="en">underboss</span></li></ol>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbaas.html>onderbaas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbazen.html>onderbazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbaas.html>onderbaasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">base</span> of a <span class="Latn" lang="en">pillar</span></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">under</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:broek.html>broek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trousers</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Attested since the seventeenth century.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbroek.html>onderbroek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbroeken.html>onderbroeken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderbroekje.html>onderbroekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a pair of undershorts, <a href = vnd.unilang:underpants.html>underpants</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:pants.html>pants</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">underwear for any sex or gender</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, short or long johns which can be worn under trousers and directly on the skin of lower limbs and private parts

<dl><dd><i>He <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> clean <b><a href = vnd.unilang:underpants.html>underpants</a></b> from the drawer.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Originated from the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderdoen.html>onderdoen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to subjugate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, this verb fell in disuse in the modern language. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">onder-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderdrukken.html>onderdrukken</a> (10605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">onderdrucken</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">onder-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drukken.html>drukken</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderdrukken.html>onderdrukken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to oppress</li>
<li>to suppress
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:troepen.html>troepen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onderdrukten.html>onderdrukten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verzet.html>verzet</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weken.html>weken</a>.</i><sup><a class="external autonumber" href="https://nl.wikipedia.org/wiki/WarschaupactGeschiedenis">[1]</a></sup>  |  The troops <b>suppressed</b> the resistance in two weeks.</dd></dl></li></ol>

***ondergaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ondergaan.html>ondergaan</a> (5560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ondergaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">onder-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergaan.html>ondergaan</a>, ondergáán</strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to undergo, endure
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onderging.html>onderging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:straf.html>straf</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>He <b>underwent</b> his punishment.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to put up with
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:herrie.html>herrie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergaan.html>ondergaan</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> want <b>to put up with</b> that noise.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergaan.html>ondergaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">  past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergaan.html>ondergaan</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ondergaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ondergrond.html>ondergrond</a> (31681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:grond.html>grond</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">underground</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Untergrund</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergrond.html>ondergrond</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergrond.html>ondergronden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondergrond.html>ondergrondje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>underground, subsoil, subsurface, bottom</li>
<li>ground, basis, foundation, groundwork</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> compartment <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">mound beneath the shield in a coat of arms on which the <a href = vnd.unilang:supporters.html>supporters</a> stand</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
